***вручать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вручать.html>вруча́ть</a> (10676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вручить.html>вручи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vručítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вручать.html>вруча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vručátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вручить.html>вручи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hand over, to deliver, to present
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вручать.html>вруча́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:орден.html>о́рден</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vručátʹ</b> komú-libo órden</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to invest/present somebody with an order</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вручать.html>вруча́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:судебный.html>суде́бную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повестка.html>пове́стку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vručátʹ</b> sudébnuju povéstku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to serve a subpoena</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to entrust
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вручать.html>вруча́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>судьбу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vručátʹ</b> svojú sudʹbú</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to entrust</b> one's destiny</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вручить.html>вручи́ть</a> (4614)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вручить.html>вручи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vručítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вручать.html>вруча́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hand over, to deliver, to present
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вручить.html>вручи́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:орден.html>о́рден</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vručítʹ</b> komú-libo órden</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to invest/present somebody with an order</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вручить.html>вручи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:судебный.html>суде́бную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повестка.html>пове́стку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vručítʹ</b> sudébnuju povéstku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to serve a subpoena</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to entrust
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вручить.html>вручи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:судьба.html>судьбу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vručítʹ</b> svojú sudʹbú</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to entrust</b> one's destiny</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:врываться.html>врыва́ться</a> (9687)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:врываться.html>врыва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vryvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ворваться.html>ворва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rush into, to burst, to enter by force, to violently or hurriedly, to intrude</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>to dig oneself into</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">врыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:всадить.html>всади́ть</a> (11869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всадить.html>всади́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vsadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всаживать.html>вса́живать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(into)</i>, to thrust <i>(into)</i>, to plunge <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:всадить.html>всади́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:пуля.html>пу́лю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лоб.html>лоб</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vsadítʹ</b> komú-libo púlju v lob</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to send a bullet through smb's head; blow out smb's brains</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend <i>(on)</i>, to pour <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:всадить.html>всади́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:огромный.html>огро́мные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>деньги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>vsadíl</b> v éto délo ogrómnyje denʹgi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has poured enormous money into that business</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***всадник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:всадник.html>вса́дник</a> (3840)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, most likely formed within Slavic from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садить.html>сади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sadítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to seat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; less likely related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">सादिन्</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sādin</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">riding, rider</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***всаживать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:всаживать.html>вса́живать</a> (29868)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всадить.html>всади́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vsadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всаживать.html>вса́живать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vsáživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всадить.html>всади́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(into)</i>, to thrust <i>(into)</i>, to plunge <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:всаживать.html>вса́живать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нож.html>нож</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спи́ну</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vsáživatʹ</b> nož v spínu komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stab smb in the back</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:всаживать.html>вса́живать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шпора.html>шпо́ры</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шади</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vsáživatʹ</b> špóry (lóšadi)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to prick horse with spurs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend <i>(on)</i>, to pour <i>(into)</i></li></ol>

<p><b>вса́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:всадить.html>всади́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-саж-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ива</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:всасывание.html>вса́сывание</a> (23697)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всасывать.html>вса́сывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vsásyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ание</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всасывание.html>вса́сывание</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vsásyvanije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всасывание.html>вса́сывания</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всасывание.html>вса́сывания</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всасывание.html>вса́сываний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>absorption, suction <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act or process of absorbing or sucking in anything</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всасывать.html>вса́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vsásyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всосать.html>всоса́ть</a></b>)

<ol><li>to suck in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:всасывать.html>вса́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>матери</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vsásyvatʹ</b> s molokóm materi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">imbibe with one's mother's milk</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to soak up, to soak in, to absorb</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всевышний.html>всевы́шний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vsevýšnij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всевышний.html>всевы́шнего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всевышний.html>всевы́шние</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всевышний.html>всевы́шних</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всевышний.html>всевы́шняя</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the Most High, the supreme God</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вы́ш<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ний</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 2*a-.
<a href = vnd.unilang:краткий.html>Кра́ткая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> муж. р. предположительна.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-вс-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-е-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-выш-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b>.
</p>

***всегда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:всегда.html>всегда́</a> (161)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> part is related to <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> meaning "all, every, the whole".
The -гда ending is also found in <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a>, see the etymology there. This ending may have derived from the genitive of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">god</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">period of time</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also годъ, <a href = vnd.unilang:тогда.html>тогда́</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всегда.html>всегда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vsegdá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>always</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>всег<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, местоименное, определительное, обстоятельственное, <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>; неизменяемое.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-всегда-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вселённый.html>вселе́н</a>(ная)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vselén(naja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вселенский.html>вселе́нский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vselénskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> universe; universal</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often  ironic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> worldwide, universal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вселенский.html>вселе́нская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорбь.html>скорбь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vselénskaja</b> skorbʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">world-weariness</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ecumenical
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вселенский.html>вселе́нский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собор.html>собо́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vselénskij</b> sobór</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>ecumenical</b> council</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вселиться.html>всели́ться</a> (19149)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вселить.html>всели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vselítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вселиться.html>всели́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vselítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вселя́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move in, to move <i>(into)</i>, to install oneself <i>(in)</i>, <i>(illegally)</i> to squat <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бес.html>бес</a>/чёрт <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вселиться.html>всели́лся</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kakoj bes/čórt v tebjá <b>vselílsja</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what's gotten into you?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take root <i>(in)</i>, to become implanted <i>(in)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вселить.html>всели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vselítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>ли́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 4b: буд. вр. — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:вселиться.html>всели́шься</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вселиться.html>всели́тся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вселиться.html>всели́мся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вселиться.html>всели́тесь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вселиться.html>вселя́тся</a></i>.
